wpb_teaser_grid_post\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2 class=\"wpb_heading wpb_teaser_grid_heading\">Wellness Articles</h2>\t\t\t<div class=\"teaser_grid_container\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"wpb_thumbnails wpb_thumbnails-fluid vc_clearfix\" data-layout-mode=\"fitRows\" style=\"position: relative; height: 817.5px;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"isotope-item vc_col-sm-12  grid-cat-1385 grid-cat-1454 grid-cat-1880 grid-cat-1929\" style=\"position: absolute; left: 0px; top: 0px;\"><div class=\"isotope-inner\">\t<h2 class=\"post-title\">\n\t\t<a href=\"https://hayliepomroy.com/cookie-craving-heres-what-to-to-do/\" class=\"link_title\" title=\"Permalink to Cookie Craving? Here’s What to To Do\">Cookie Craving? Here’s What to To Do</a>\t</h2>\n\t<div class=\"post-thumb\">\n\t\t<a href=\"https://hayliepomroy.com/cookie-craving-heres-what-to-to-do/\" class=\"link_image\" title=\"Permalink to Cookie Craving? Here’s What to To Do\"><img width=\"150\" height=\"150\" src=\"https://d3ctlfpe85j9pf.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/Tahini_Oatmeal_Cookies-150x150.jpeg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail\" alt=\"Tahini Oatmeal Cookies\"></a>\t</div>\n\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\tDo you find yourself reaching for the cookie jar in the afternoon? Food cravings — like a hankering for pastries and bread — are one way our bodies communicate with us. Don’t blame your will power; a craving for bread, cookies and muffins can be a clue that your body isn’t getting what it needs. […]<!-- e-->\t</div>\n\t<a href=\"https://hayliepomroy.com/cookie-craving-heres-what-to-to-do/\" class=\"vc_read_more\" title=\"Permalink to Cookie Craving?
